    <script>
        function toggleAriaExpanded() {
            if (document.getElementById("province-selector-popup").style.display == 'none') {
                $("#province-selector-trigger").attr('aria-expanded', "false");
            }
            else {
                $("#province-selector-trigger").attr('aria-expanded', "true");
            }
            return true;
        }
        let timer = setInterval(function () {
            toggleAriaExpanded();
        }, 500);
    </script>

            <script>
                $(document).ready(function () {
                    var linksRight = '.global-navigation.gn-shop.bell-aliant .federal-bar-links.federal-bar-links_right .header-preferences .footer-header-preferences-buttons ul li.fed-links a.trigger-popup, .global-navigation.bell-aliant .federal-bar-links_right li.fed-start a';
                    var linksRightOther = '.global-navigation.gn-shop .federal-bar-links.federal-bar-links_right .header-preferences .footer-header-preferences-buttons ul li.fed-links a.trigger-popup, .global-navigation.gn-shop .federal-bar-links_right  li.fed-start a';
                    $(document).on('click', linksRight, function () {
                        $(linksRight).attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
                        $(linksRight).next('div').css('display', 'none');
                        $(this).attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
                        $(this).next('div').css('display', 'block');
                    });
                    $(document).on('click', linksRightOther, function () {
                        $(linksRightOther).attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
                        $(linksRightOther).next('div').css('display', 'none');
                        $(this).attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
                        $(this).next('div').css('display', 'block');
                    });

                    $(document).on('focusin', linksRightOther, linksRight, function () {
                        $(linksRightOther).add(linksRight).attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
                        $(linksRightOther).add(linksRight).next('div').css('display', 'none');
                    });
                });
            </script>
        </div>
    </div>
    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
            $('.store-locator-filter-checkbox').on('keypress', function (event) {
                if (event.which === 13) {
                    this.checked = !this.checked;
                }
            });
        });
    </script>

<script>
    //shop1
    $(document).on("keydown", function (event) {
        var aa = $('.connector-area.rsx-active');
        var link = $("leftnavbtn_7");
        if (event.keyCode === 32 && $(document.activeElement).is(link)) {
            event.preventDefault();
            link.trigger("click");
            aa.trigger("click");
            window.location.href = link.attr("href");
        }
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    $(function () {

  function getCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
      var c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
        c = c.substring(1);
      }
      if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
        return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
      }
    }
    return "";
        }

  function getUrlVars(cvalue) {
    var vars = {};
    if (!cvalue) return vars;
    var parts = cvalue.replace(/([^=&]+)=([^&]*)/gi, function (m, key, value) {
      vars[key] = value;
    });
    return vars;
  }

  //console.log("ready!");
  var bsccCookie = getCookie("BSCC");
  if (!bsccCookie) {
    return;
  }

  //console.log(bsccCookie);
  var bsccCookieValues = getUrlVars(bsccCookie);
  if (!bsccCookieValues) {
    return;
  }

  //console.info(bsccCookieValues);

        var totalCartItems = parseInt(bsccCookieValues["totalcartitems_QC"]);
  if (!isNaN(totalCartItems)) {
    //console.info(totalCartItems);
    if(totalCartItems){
      $(".shopping-cart-button .connector-cart-count").removeClass("sr-only");
      $(".shopping-cart-button .connector-cart-count").text(totalCartItems);
    }
    else{
      $(".shopping-cart-button .connector-cart-count").addClass("sr-only");
    }
  }

});
</script>

    <div class="g-connector-desktop-nav-backdrop" id="connectorNavBackdropDesktop" style="height: 0"></div>
</div>

<script>
    document.onkeydown = function(evt) {
        evt = evt || window.event;
        if (evt.keyCode == 27) {
            var removeClasses = document.querySelectorAll('.shimmer');
            removeClasses.forEach(function(el) {
                el.classList.remove("shimmer");
                sessionStorage.setItem("removeShimmer", "yes");
            })
        }
    };

    if(sessionStorage.getItem("removeShimmer") == "yes"){
        var removeClasses = document.querySelectorAll('.shimmer');
        removeClasses.forEach(function(el) {
        el.classList.remove("shimmer");
            sessionStorage.setItem("removeShimmer", "yes");
        })
    }
</script>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

        var ul = document.querySelectorAll('.change-region-list');
        var changeButton = document.querySelectorAll(".change-region-link")
        var liSelected;
        var index = 0;
        ul.forEach((elem, i) => {
            elem.querySelectorAll('input').forEach((e, i) => {
                e.addEventListener('keydown', function (et) {
                    var KeyID = et.key;
                    switch (KeyID) {
                        case "Enter":
                        case " ":
                            e.click();
                            break;
                        default:
                            break;
                    }
                });
            });
            elem.addEventListener('focus', (event) => {
                elem.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
            });
            elem.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
                var len = elem.getElementsByTagName('li').length - 1;
                if ((index == len && event.which === 9 && !event.shiftKey) || (index == 0 && (event.which === 9 && event.shiftKey))) {
                    return;
                }
                if (event.which === 40 || (event.which === 9 && !event.shiftKey)) {
                    index++;
                    //down
                    if (liSelected) {
                        next = elem.getElementsByTagName('li')[index];
                        if (typeof next !== undefined && index <= len) {
                            liSelected = next;
                            if (liSelected.querySelector("input").hasAttribute("disabled")) {
                                index++;
                                next = elem.getElementsByTagName('li')[index];
                                liSelected = next;
                            }
                        } else {
                            index = 0;
                            liSelected = elem.getElementsByTagName('li')[index];
                        }
                        liSelected.querySelector("input").focus();
                    } else {
                        index = 1;
                        liSelected = elem.getElementsByTagName('li')[index];
                        liSelected.querySelector("input").focus();
                    }
                    event.preventDefault();
                } else if (event.which === 38 || (event.which === 9 && event.shiftKey)) {
                    //up
                    if (liSelected) {
                        index--;
                        liSelected.querySelector("input").focus();
                        next = elem.getElementsByTagName('li')[index];
                        if (typeof next !== undefined && index >= 0) {
                            liSelected = next;
                            liSelected = elem.getElementsByTagName('li')[index];
                            liSelected.querySelector("input").focus();
                            if (liSelected.querySelector("input").hasAttribute("disabled")) {
                                index--;
                                next = elem.getElementsByTagName('li')[index];
                                liSelected = next;
                                liSelected.querySelector("input").focus();
                            }
                        } else {
                            index = len;
                            liSelected = elem.getElementsByTagName('li')[len];
                            liSelected.querySelector("input").focus();
                        }
                    } else {
                        index = 1;
                        liSelected = elem.getElementsByTagName('li')[len];
                        liSelected.querySelector("input").focus();
                    }
                    event.preventDefault();
                }
            }, false);

        });

        changeButton.forEach((elem, i) => {
            elem.addEventListener('focus', (event) => {
                index = 0;
            });
            elem.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
                if (event.which === 9 && !event.shiftKey && ((elem.getAttribute("aria-expanded") === "true") || !document.querySelector("#changeRegionBoxMobile").classList.contains("change-region-hidden"))) {
                    ul[i].getElementsByTagName('li')[0].querySelector('input').focus();
                    event.preventDefault();
                }

                if ((event.which === 13) && document.querySelector("#changeRegionBoxMobile").classList.contains("change-region-hidden")) {
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        document.querySelector(".mobileCloseButton").focus();
                    }, 100)
                }

            });

            elem.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
                if (document.querySelector("#changeRegionBoxMobile").classList.contains("change-region-hidden")) {
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        document.querySelector(".mobileCloseButton").focus();
                    }, 100)
                }

            });
        });

        document.querySelector(".mobileCloseButton").addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
            if (event.which === 9) {
                index = 0;
                document.querySelector("#changeRegionBoxMobile").querySelector("ul").getElementsByTagName('li')[0].querySelector('input').focus();
                event.preventDefault();
            }
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var promoTagHeader = document.getElementById("promoTagHeader");
        if (promoTagHeader) {
            var fixedNav = document.getElementById("fixedHeader");
            var promoFixed = promoTagHeader.offsetTop;

            stickyHeaderScroll();
            //remove sticky once close button is clicked
            $('.js-promoTagClose').on('click', function (e) {
                promoTagHeader.classList.add('stickyPromoTag');
                e.preventDefault();
            });

            window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
                stickyHeaderScroll();
                if (window.pageYOffset > promoFixed) {
                    promoTagHeader.classList.add("fixed-promo-tag");

                    if(fixedNav){
                        var fixedNavHeight = fixedNav.offsetHeight;
                        promoTagHeader.style.top = fixedNavHeight +"px";
                    }
                } else {
                    promoTagHeader.classList.remove("fixed-promo-tag");
                    promoTagHeader.style.top = 0 + "px";
                }
            });
        }
    });

    function stickyHeaderScroll() {
        let promoStickyCloseBtn = document.querySelectorAll('.js-promoTagClose');
        if (promoStickyCloseBtn.length > 0) {
            promoStickyCloseBtn.forEach(function (index) {
                //prevent display on load
                index.classList.remove('d-none');
                let promoTag = index.closest('#promoTagHeader');
                let promoPosition = window.getComputedStyle(promoTag).getPropertyValue('position');
                //check if position is still sticky to display close button
                if ((document.body.scrollTop > 20 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 20) && promoPosition == 'sticky') {
                    index.style.display = "inline";
                } else {
                    index.style.display = "none";
                }
            });
        }
    }

    function getSocInformation() {
        try {
            $('body').loadingIndicator();
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                headers: {
                    'brand': 'B',
                    'Province': 'QC',
                    "accept-language": 'en'
                },
                url: "https://apigate.bell.ca/uxpcommon/UXP.Services/Common/PDM/GetProductsByIdentifier",
                data: {
                    "TranslateIds": [] ,
                    "TranslateIdentifierType": "SOC"
                },
                success: function (data) {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        data: { "promoSocInfo": data },
                        url: "/EShop/Qualification/GetSocDetails",
                        success: function (response) {
                            $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                            $('#promo-code-modal-body').html(response);
                            $('#promo-code').modal('show');
                        },
                        error: function (err) {
                            $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                            $('#modal-error-occured').modal('show');
                        }
                    });
                }
            });

        } catch (e) {
            $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
            $('#modal-error-occured').modal('show');
        }
    }


    $(document).ready(function () {
        /* OPEN */
        $('#promo-code').on('shown.bs.modal', function () {
            $('#promo-code-banner-close-btn').focus();
        });

        /* CLOSE */
        $('#promo-code').on('hide.bs.modal', function () {
            $('#promoTagHeader-view-offers').focus();
        });
    });
</script>

        $("#eShopAddressModal1").modal();
    }

    function urlParam(name) {
        var results = new RegExp('[\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)').exec(window.location.href);
        if (results == null) {
            return null;
        }
        else {
            return decodeURI(results[1]) || 0;
        }
    }
    });

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var hideSessionTimeout = true;
var idleTime = 1000; // in msec
var sessionTimeOutInSeconds = 900; //15 minutes

var sessionTimer;
var countStartTime;
var countCurrentTime;
var countdownTimeDiffSec;
var countdownTimeDiffSecLeft = sessionTimeOutInSeconds;
var isTimingOutOmnitureCalled = false;
var isTimedOutOmnitureCalled = false;
var timeExpired = false;

$(document).ready(function () {

	countStartTime = new Date(Date.now());

    sessionTimer = setTimeout('sessionCountDown()', idleTime);
	
    $('.session-modal').on('shown.bs.modal', function () {
        var firstFocusableElement;
        var lastFocusableElement;
        var newModal = $(this);
        var focusableContent = $(newModal).find('a[href], button, input, textarea, select, details, *[tabindex]').not('[tabindex=-1], :hidden');
        if (focusableContent.length > 0) {
            firstFocusableElement = focusableContent[0];
            lastFocusableElement = focusableContent[focusableContent.length - 1];
        }
        $(firstFocusableElement).focus();
        $(newModal).keydown(function (e) {
            if ((e.which || e.keyCode) == 9) {
                if ($(lastFocusableElement).is(":focus") && (e.shiftKey == false)) {
                    $(firstFocusableElement).focus();
                    e.preventDefault();
                }
                else if ($(firstFocusableElement).is(":focus") && (e.shiftKey == true)) {
                    $(lastFocusableElement).focus();
                    e.preventDefault();
                }
            }
        });
    });

});

	
function updateCounterInPopup() {
	
	tim = secondsToTime(countdownTimeDiffSecLeft)
	$('#session-modal-timer').html(twoDigit(tim.m) + ":" + twoDigit(tim.s));
    if (tim.s == 0) {
        $('#session-modal-timer-sr span').html(tim.m);
    }
}

function secondsToTime(secs) {
	secs = Math.round(secs);
	var hours = Math.floor(secs / (60 * 60));

	var divisor_for_minutes = secs % (60 * 60);
	var minutes = Math.floor(divisor_for_minutes / 60);

	var divisor_for_seconds = divisor_for_minutes % 60;
	var seconds = Math.ceil(divisor_for_seconds);

	var obj = {
		"h": hours,
		"m": minutes,
		"s": seconds
	};
	return obj;
}

function twoDigit(num) {
	var twodigit = num >= 10 ? num : "0" + num.toString();
	return twodigit;
}


function sessionCountDown() {

	countCurrentTime = getTime();

	countdownTimeDiffSec = getTimeDifferenceInSeconds(); 
	countdownTimeDiffSecLeft = sessionTimeOutInSeconds - countdownTimeDiffSec;
			
    if (countdownTimeDiffSec >= 2*sessionTimeOutInSeconds/3 && countdownTimeDiffSec < sessionTimeOutInSeconds) {	

        $("#session-modal-expiring").modal({ backdrop: 'static', keyboard: false, show: true });

		updateCounterInPopup();

        if (isTimingOutOmnitureCalled == false) {
            isTimingOutOmnitureCalled = true;

            //omniture
            if (typeof s_oTrackPage != 'undefined') {
                var lightboxTitle = $("#session-modal-expiring h2").text();
                var lightboxContent = $("#session-modal-expiring p").text().substring(0, 100);
                var lightboxMsg = $("#session-modal-expiring p").text().replace(/([\:\,\[\]\'\"])/g, '').substring(0, 48);
                s_oTrackPage({
                    s_oAPT: "104-2-2",
                    s_oPRM: "open, ".concat(lightboxTitle),
                    s_oLBC: lightboxContent,
                    s_oPLE: lightboxMsg.concat(":c")
                });
            }
        }
	}
	else if (countdownTimeDiffSec >= sessionTimeOutInSeconds) {
        sessionTimedOut = true;
        timeExpired = true;
	
		$("#session-modal-expiring").modal('hide');

        var language = $("#language").val();
        if (window.location.href.indexOf("/Bell-bundles/Checkout") > -1 || window.location.href.indexOf("/Forfaits-Bell/Caisse") > -1) {
            ClearAddressOnSessionTimeout(language == "en" ? "/Bell-bundles" : "/Forfaits-Bell")
        }
        else {
            if (isTimedOutOmnitureCalled == false) {
                isTimedOutOmnitureCalled = true;
                //omniture
                if (typeof s_oTrackPage != 'undefined') {
                    var lightboxTitle = $("#session-modal-expiring h2").text();
                    var lightboxContent = $("#session-modal-expiring p").text().substring(0, 100);
                    var lightboxMsg = $("#session-modal-expiring p").text().replace(/([\:\,\[\]\'\"])/g, '').substring(0, 48);
                    s_oTrackPage({
                        s_oAPT: "104-2-2",
                        s_oPRM: "open, ".concat(lightboxTitle),
                        s_oLBC: lightboxContent,
                        s_oPLE: lightboxMsg.concat(":e")
                    });
                }
            }
            $("#session-modal-expired").modal({ backdrop: 'static', keyboard: false, show: true });
        }
	}
	
	if (countdownTimeDiffSec <= sessionTimeOutInSeconds) {
		sessionTimer = setTimeout('sessionCountDown()', idleTime);
	}
}

//Added code to count time between page load (start time) and current time after screen awake. Jira defect# BELLCAQP-793
function getTime() {
	var timeNow = new Date();
	return timeNow;
}

//Added code to count time between page load (start time) and current time after screen awake. Jira defect# BELLCAQP-793
function getTimeDifferenceInSeconds() {
	var msec = countCurrentTime - countStartTime;
	var sec = Math.floor(msec / 1000);
	return sec;
}

function reloadFrame() {

	countStartTime = getTime();
	countdownTimeDiffSecLeft = sessionTimeOutInSeconds
	
	$('#session-modal-timer').removeClass('txtRed');
    $("#session-modal-expiring").modal('hide');
    $.ajax({
        url: window.location.origin+"/EShop/CheckOut/KeepSessionAlive",
        success: function (data) {
            if (data.Success) {
                //clearTimeout(sessionTimeOutInSeconds);
                $('#session-modal-timer').removeClass('txtRed');
                sessionTimer = setTimeout('sessionCountDown()', idleTime); // 10 min timer for the lightbox to reappear.
            }
        }
    });
}

function reloadFrameNew() {
    countStartTime = getTime();
    countdownTimeDiffSecLeft = sessionTimeOutInSeconds

    //varStatusReport2 = varStatusReport2 + "</br>ReloadFrame() Start Time: " + countStartTime;
    //$('#dateTimeDisplay2').html(varStatusReport2);

    $('#session-modal-timer').removeClass('txtRed');
    $("#session-modal-expiring").modal('hide');

    $.ajax({
        url: "/Order/KeepSessionAlive",
        success: function (data) {
            if (data.Success) {
                //clearTimeout(sessionTimeOutInSeconds);
                $('#session-modal-timer').removeClass('txtRed');
                sessionTimer = setTimeout('sessionCountDown()', idleTime); // 10 min timer for the lightbox to reappear.
            }
        }
    });
}

function ClearAddressOnSessionTimeout(strURL) {

    $.ajax({
        url: "/EShop/Qualification/ClearAddressOnSessionTimeout",
        success: function (data) {
            if (data.Success) {

            }

            if (strURL != undefined)
                window.location.href = strURL;
            else
                window.location.reload();
        }
    });
}

function checkSesstionTimeout() {
    $("#session-modal-expired").modal({ backdrop: 'static', keyboard: false, show: true });
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    window.addEventListener('load', function () {
        console.log("CentralQualModals called...");

            var link = document.createElement("link");
            link.rel = "stylesheet";
            link.href = "https://ws1.postescanada-canadapost.ca/css/addresscomplete-2.30.min.css?key=XP67-TU34-DZ98-EE18";
            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(link);

            $.getScript("https://ws1.postescanada-canadapost.ca/js/addresscomplete-2.30.min.js?key=XP67-TU34-DZ98-EE18")
            .done(function( script, textStatus ) {

                var isLoadingModals = true;
                var modalQueue;

                (function ($) {
                    if (typeof $ !== 'undefined') {
                        var centralQualParams = {
                            gigabitPreFlow: '',
                            shopQualModal: true,
                            resPath: '/BRSeShop/qualification/central_shop_internet',
                            returnUrl: window.location.href,
                            framework: "brf"
                        };

                        $.ajax({
                            type: 'GET',
                    url: '/eShop/Qualification/HowtoBuyInternet',
                            data: centralQualParams,
                            success: function (data) {

                                $('#centralQual').html(data);
                                isLoadingModals = false;
                                $('body').loadingIndicator();
                                $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                                $(modalQueue).click();
                                $("#centralQual").trigger("centralQualLoaded");
                            },
                            error: function (xhr, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                                $('body').loadingIndicator();
                                $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                                console.log("Cannot load");
                                isLoadingModals = false;
                            }
                        });

                $(".qualPrdSet").on("click", function () {
                    $("#qualPrd").val($(this).data("product-name"));
                    $("#qualPrdShortName").val($(this).data("product-shortname"));
                    $("#qualPrdLob").val($(this).data("product-lobname"));
                    $("#qualOffers").val($(this).data("offers"));
                    if ($(this).next().hasClass("internetPackagePromoCode")) {
                        $("#qualPromoCode").val($(this).next().val());
                    }
                });

                var oldAddbtnURL = ""; 
                $(".customOrdeNowBtn").on("click", function () {
                    var shortName = $(this).data("product-shortname");
                    var lobName = $(this).data("product-lobname");
                    var productId = $(this).data("product-id");
                    if (shortName !== "" && shortName !== 'undefined' && shortName !== undefined && shortName !== null
                        && lobName !== "" && lobName !== 'undefined' && lobName != undefined && lobName !== null
                        && productId !== "" && productId !== 'undefined' && productId != undefined && productId !== null) {
                        var addServiceButtonId = "";
                        if (lobName === "SHOP_INTERNET") {
                            addServiceButtonId = "#Add_Internet" + productId;
                        } else if (lobName === "SATELLITE_TV") {
                            addServiceButtonId = "#Add_Satellite" + productId;
                        }
                        var $link = $(addServiceButtonId);
                        if (oldAddbtnURL === '' || oldAddbtnURL === 'undefined') {
                            oldAddbtnURL = "https://mybell.bell.ca/Login?refreshLink=https://www.bell.ca/existingCustomerRedirect%3FUrlReferrer=/Bell_Internet/Internet_access";
                        }
                        var newUrl = oldAddbtnURL + "%26LobType=" + shortName + "%26ShortName=" + lobName;
                        $link.attr("href", newUrl);
                    }
                });

                $("#centralQualButton").on("click", function () {
                    $("#qualPrd").val("");
                    $("#qualOffers").val("");
                });
                $('#centralQualButton, .qualPrdSet, .qual-force-fibe-availability').on('click', function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var postQualFlag = typeof $(this).attr("data-post-qual") != undefined ? $(this).data('post-qual') : true;
                    if (!postQualFlag) {
                            if (isLoadingModals) {
                                $('body').loadingIndicator({
                                    message: $("#divloadertext").text(),
                                    template: ''
                                });
                                modalQueue = this;
                            }
                    }
                        });

                    } else {
                        console.log('Cannot load script');
                    }

                    if ($("body").hasClass("page-code_prsshppns-landing")) {

                        $("body").on("click", ".js-omni-button", function () {

                            var variables = {
                                s_oLBC: $(this).data("omni-s_olbc"),
                                s_oPRM: $(this).data("omni-s_oprm"),
                                s_oAPT: $(this).data("omni-s_oapt"),
                                s_oBTN: $(this).data("omni-s_obtn")
                            }

                            if (typeof $(this).data("omni-s_obrsqualtype") !== "undefined") {
                                variables.s_oBRSQualType = $(this).data("omni-s_obrsqualtype");
                            }

                            if (typeof (s_oTrackPage) !== "undefined") {
                                s_oTrackPage(variables);
                            }
                        });
                    }
                })($);
            });


        });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).on('click', '#CMB_submit_1', function (e) {

        var self = BELL.rsx.callMeBack,
            _$ = this._$,
            formValid = true,
            form = e.currentTarget,
            onFalure = function (result) {
                $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                $("#CMB_errorDiv_Request").removeClass('hide');
                $('#cmbSuccessMessage').addClass('hide');
                s_oTrackPage({
                    s_oAPT: "197-2-2",
                    s_oARS: "CLNTERR-50001",
                    s_oERR_CLASS: "CLNTERR-50001:[T|BE]",
                    s_oERR_DESC: "CLNTERR-50001:could not process form data",
                    s_oPLE: FormatLightBoxContent($("#CMB_errorDiv_Request").text()) + ":E[LNTERR-50001]"
                });
            };

        omitureErrorNumberList = [];
        omitureErrorClassList = [];
        omitureErrorDescriptionList = [];
        omitureErrorRequiredList = []; omitureErrorInvalidList = [];

        //Do not submit automatically
        e.preventDefault();
        //Reset all the error messages
        //self._resetErrors();

        formValid = isFormValid();
        //only submit the data if it's all valid
        if (formValid) {
            //Submit data here
            $('#UserAction').val("CMB_Submit_Success");
            //Show loading indicator
            $('body').loadingIndicator('show');
            //Silent save form data
            self.save(function (result) {
                //On success
                //Hide loading indicator
                $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                //Check the response
                if (result == "True") {
                    //Brownfield FTTH – CR-012 – Omniture reporting
                    s_oTrackPage({
                        s_oAPT: "197-2-1",
                        s_oPLE: FormatLightBoxContent($("#cmbSuccessMessage").text()) + ":C"
                    });
                    $("#cmbSuccessMessage").removeClass('hide');
                    self.hide();
                } else onFalure(result);
            }, function (result) {
                //On falure
                console.log("Submit failure");
                onFalure(result);
                //Hide loading indicator
                $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                //If response required a redirect - do the redirect
                if (result.responseJSON != undefined && result.responseJSON.RedirectToPage) {
                    window.location.replace(result.responseJSON.RedirectToPage);
                }
                console.log(result);
            });
        } else {
            var onmi = {
                s_oAPT: "197-2-2",
                s_oARS: omitureErrorNumberList.join(","),
                s_oERR_CLASS: omitureErrorClassList.join(","),
                s_oERR_DESC: omitureErrorDescriptionList.join(","),
                s_oPLE: ""
            };
            if (omitureErrorRequiredList.length) onmi.s_oPLE += "required info:E:[" + omitureErrorRequiredList.join(",") + "]";
            if (omitureErrorRequiredList.length && omitureErrorInvalidList.length) onmi.s_oPLE += ",";
            if (omitureErrorInvalidList.length) onmi.s_oPLE += "invalid entry:E:[" + omitureErrorInvalidList.join(",") + "]";
            s_oTrackPage(onmi);
            return false;
        }

        return true;
    });

    var isFormValid = function () {
        var CMB_name = $('#CMB_name').val();
        var CMB_phone = $('#CMB_phone').val();
        var CMB_extention = $('#CMB_extention').val();
        var CMB_email = $('#CMB_email').val();
        var isError = false;
        $(".CMB_required_name").addClass("hide");
        $(".CMB_invalid_name").addClass("hide");
        $(".CMB_required_phone").addClass("hide");
        $(".CMB_invalid_phone").addClass("hide");
        $(".CMB_required_email").addClass("hide");
        $(".CMB_invalid_email").addClass("hide");

        if (CMB_name === "") {
            $(".CMB_required_name").removeClass("hide");
            isError = true;
            omniErrors = omnitureErrorCodes["CMB_name"];
            omitureErrorNumberList.push(omniErrors.required.code);
            omitureErrorClassList.push(omniErrors.required.code + ":[V|FE]");
            omitureErrorDescriptionList.push(omniErrors.required.code + ":" + omniErrors.required.desc);
            omitureErrorRequiredList.push(omniErrors.required.code);
        } else {
            $(".CMB_required_name").addClass("hide");

            if (/^(?:[A-Za-z\u00C0-\u017F\-\s\'\`\.]){1,}(?:\s[A-Za-z\u00C0-\u017F\-\s\'\`\.]{1,})+$/.test(CMB_name) === false) {
                $(".CMB_invalid_name").removeClass("hide");
                isError = true;
                omniErrors = omnitureErrorCodes["CMB_name"];
                omitureErrorNumberList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code);
                omitureErrorClassList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code + ":[V|FE]");
                omitureErrorDescriptionList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code + ":" + omniErrors.invalid.desc);
                omitureErrorInvalidList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code);
            } else {
                $(".CMB_invalid_name").addClass("hide");
            }
        }

        if (CMB_phone === "") {
            $(".CMB_required_phone").removeClass("hide");
            isError = true;
            omniErrors = omnitureErrorCodes["CMB_phone"];
            omitureErrorNumberList.push(omniErrors.required.code);
            omitureErrorClassList.push(omniErrors.required.code + ":[V|FE]");
            omitureErrorDescriptionList.push(omniErrors.required.code + ":" + omniErrors.required.desc);
            omitureErrorRequiredList.push(omniErrors.required.code);
        } else {
            $(".CMB_required_phone").addClass("hide");

            if (/^\d{10}$/.test(CMB_phone) === false) {
                $(".CMB_invalid_phone").removeClass("hide");
                isError = true;
                omniErrors = omnitureErrorCodes["CMB_phone"];
                omitureErrorNumberList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code);
                omitureErrorClassList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code + ":[V|FE]");
                omitureErrorDescriptionList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code + ":" + omniErrors.invalid.desc);
                omitureErrorInvalidList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code);
            } else {
                $(".CMB_invalid_phone").addClass("hide");
            }
        }

        if (CMB_email === "") {
            $(".CMB_required_email").removeClass("hide");
            isError = true;
            omniErrors = omnitureErrorCodes["CMB_email"];
            omitureErrorNumberList.push(omniErrors.required.code);
            omitureErrorClassList.push(omniErrors.required.code + ":[V|FE]");
            omitureErrorDescriptionList.push(omniErrors.required.code + ":" + omniErrors.required.desc);
            omitureErrorRequiredList.push(omniErrors.required.code);
        } else {
            $(".CMB_required_email").addClass("hide");

            if (/^[a-z0-9A-Z](([-_.~]|(\.\.))?[a-z0-9A-Z])*\u0040[a-z0-9A-Z]([-.]?[a-z0-9A-Z])*\.([A-Za-z]{2,})$/.test(CMB_email) === false) {
                $(".CMB_invalid_email").removeClass("hide");
                isError = true;
                omniErrors = omnitureErrorCodes["CMB_email"];
                omitureErrorNumberList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code);
                omitureErrorClassList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code + ":[V|FE]");
                omitureErrorDescriptionList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code + ":" + omniErrors.invalid.desc);
                omitureErrorInvalidList.push(omniErrors.invalid.code);
            } else {
                $(".CMB_invalid_email").addClass("hide");
            }
        }

        return !isError;
    };

    var omnitureErrorCodes = {
        'CMB_name': {
            required: {
                code: 'CLNTERR-011',
                desc: 'name is required'
            },
            invalid: {
                code: 'CLNTERR-012',
                desc: 'name is invalid'
            }
        },
        'CMB_phone': {
            required: {
                code: 'CLNTERR-021',
                desc: 'phone is required'
            },
            invalid: {
                code: 'CLNTERR-022',
                desc: 'phone is invalid'
            }
        },
        'CMB_extention': {
            required: {
                code: 'CLNTERR-031',
                desc: 'phone extention is required'
            },
            invalid: {
                code: 'CLNTERR-032',
                desc: 'phone extention is invalid'
            }
        },
        'CMB_email': {
            required: {
                code: 'CLNTERR-041',
                desc: 'email is required'
            },
            invalid: {
                code: 'CLNTERR-042',
                desc: 'email is invalid'
            }
        }
    }, omitureErrorNumberList, omitureErrorClassList, omitureErrorDescriptionList, omitureErrorRequiredList, omitureErrorInvalidList;

    function RefreshPage() {
        var getloadertext1 = jQRSX("#divloadertext").text();
        jQRSX('body').loadingIndicator({
            message: getloadertext1
        });
        jQRSX('body').loadingIndicator('show');
        // force reload when pageUrl have anchor point in the page
        window.location.reload();
    }
</script>

        //jQRSX(document).ready(function () {

        function isAlphaNumberKey(evt) {
            var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
            if (!((event.keyCode >= 65) && (event.keyCode <= 90) || (event.keyCode >= 97) && (event.keyCode <= 122) || (event.keyCode >= 48) && (event.keyCode <= 57)))
                return false;
            return true;
        }
    </script>

<!-- Request a callback light boxwith success and error light boxes -->



<script>
    if (!EShop) var EShop = {};

    EShop.RequestaCallback = (function () {

        var errors = {
            nameRequired: { field: "name", type: "required", label: "requestNameLabel", errorDiv: "errorDivRequestName", input: "request_name" },
            nameInvalid: { field: "name", type: "invalid", label: "requestNameLabel", errorDiv: "errorDivInvalidRequestName", input: "request_name" },
            numberRequired: { field: "number", type: "required", label: "requestContactLabel", errorDiv: "errorDivRequestContactNumber", input: "request_contact" },
            numberInvalid: { field: "number", type: "invalid", label: "requestContactLabel", errorDiv: "errorDivInvalidRequestContactNumber", input: "request_contact" }
        };

        function ClearExistingErrors() {
            Object.keys(errors).forEach(function (key) {
                $("#" + errors[key].errorDiv).hide();
                $("#" + errors[key].label).removeClass("rsx-txt-red");
                $("#requestCallback_modal_body").find("label").removeClass("rsx-txt-red");
                $(".rsx-txt-red").hide();
            });
        }

        var fillSuccessCallmeBackForm = function () {
            var name = $('#request_name').val();
            var contactNumber = $('#request_contact').val();
            $('#formSuccessName').text(name);
            $('#formSuccessContactNumber').text(GetFormatedPhoneNumber(contactNumber));
        }

        function GetFormatedPhoneNumber(contactNumber) {
            contactNumber = insertCharIntoStrAtPosition(' ', contactNumber, 3);//000 0000000
            contactNumber = insertCharIntoStrAtPosition('-', contactNumber, 7);//000 000-0000
            return contactNumber;
        }

        function insertCharIntoStrAtPosition(char, str, position) {
            var partBeforeChar = str.slice(0, position);
            var partAfterChar = str.slice(position);
            return [partBeforeChar,
                char,
                partAfterChar].join('');
        }

        function ShowValidationErrors(validationErrors) {
            $("#request_name").attr('aria-describedby', '');
            $("#request_contact").attr('aria-describedby', '');

            if (validationErrors.length > 0)
                $("#" + validationErrors[0].input).focus();

            for (var i = 0; i < validationErrors.length; i++) {
                var isAlreadyVisible = false;
                for (var j = 0; j < i; j++) {
                    if (validationErrors[i].field === validationErrors[j].field)
                        isAlreadyVisible = true;
                }
                if (!isAlreadyVisible) {
                    $("#" + validationErrors[i].input).attr('aria-describedby', validationErrors[i].errorDiv);
                    $("#" + validationErrors[i].errorDiv).removeClass("hide");
                    $("#" + validationErrors[i].errorDiv).show();
                    $("#" + validationErrors[i].label).addClass("rsx-txt-red");
                }
            }
        }

        function ClearCallbackErrors() {
            jQRSX("#requestCallback_modal_body").find("label").removeClass("rsx-txt-red");
            jQRSX('.rsx-txt-red').hide(); // hide all validations
        }

        var isCallMeBackFormValid = function () {
            var validationErrors = [];

            var nameError = getValidationErrorForName();
            if (nameError)
                validationErrors.push(nameError);

            var contactNumberError = getValidationErrorForContactNumber();
            if (contactNumberError)
                validationErrors.push(contactNumberError);


            ClearExistingErrors();
            ShowValidationErrors(validationErrors);

            return validationErrors.length === 0;
        };

        function getValidationErrorForName() {
            var name = jQRSX('#request_name').val();
            var regExName = /^\d*[a-zA-ZàâçéèêëîïôûùüÿñæœÀÂÇÉÈÊËÎÏÔÛÙÜŸÑÆŒ ][a-zA-Z0-9àâçéèêëîïôûùüÿñæœÀÂÇÉÈÊËÎÏÔÛÙÜŸÑÆŒ .'-]{0,39}$/;

            if (name.trim() === "")
                return errors.nameRequired;
            if (!regExName.test(name))
                return errors.nameInvalid
            return null;
        }

        function getValidationErrorForContactNumber() {
            var contactnumber = jQRSX('#request_contact').val();
            var regExContactNumber = /^\d{10}$/;

            if (contactnumber.trim() === "")
                return errors.numberRequired;
            if (!regExContactNumber.test(contactnumber))
                return errors.numberInvalid
            return null;
        }

        var setServerValidationMessages = function (serverErrors) {
            ClearExistingErrors();
            var validationErrors = [];

            serverErrors.forEach(function (serverError) {
                if (serverError.toLowerCase().indexOf("name") != -1) {
                    if (serverError.toLowerCase().indexOf("required") != -1) {
                        validationErrors.push(errors.nameRequired);
                    }
                    if (serverError.toLowerCase().indexOf("valid") != -1) {
                        validationErrors.push(errors.nameInvalid);
                    }
                }
                if (serverError.toLowerCase().indexOf("number") != -1) {
                    if (serverError.toLowerCase().indexOf("required") != -1) {
                        validationErrors.push(errors.numberRequired);
                    }
                    if (serverError.toLowerCase().indexOf("valid") != -1) {
                        validationErrors.push(errors.numberInvalid);
                    }
                }
            });
            ShowValidationErrors(validationErrors);
        }


        function isAlphaNumberKey(evt) {
            var charCode = (evt.which) ? evt.which : event.keyCode;
            if (!((event.keyCode >= 65) && (event.keyCode <= 90) || (event.keyCode >= 97) && (event.keyCode <= 122) || (event.keyCode >= 48) && (event.keyCode <= 57)))
                return false;
            return true;
        }

        function saveCallbackAddressError() {
            $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
            $('#requestCallback').modal('hide');
            $('#callmebackrequestsuccess').modal('hide');
            $('#eShopTextErrorModal5').modal();


            var lightboxContent = document.getElementById('eShopTextErrorModal5');
            lightboxContent = $(lightboxContent).text();
            try {
                s_oTrackPage({
                    s_oAPT: "104-2-2",
                    s_oPRM: "open, " + FormatLightBoxContent($("#eShopTextErrorModal5").find("h3").text()),
                    s_oLBC: Formatted_Omniture_LBContent($("#eShopTextErrorModal5").find(".rsx-notification").text()),
                    s_oARS: "CLNTERR-50001",
                    s_oERR_CLASS: "CLNTERR-50001:[T|BE]",
                    s_oERR_DESC: "CLNTERR-50001:could not process request call back form",
                    s_oPLE: FormatLightBoxContent(lightboxContent) + ":E[LNTERR-50001]"
                });
            }
            catch (e) {
            }
            return false;
        }

        var init = function () {
            $("#requestCallbackButton").click(function (event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                if (isCallMeBackFormValid()) {

                    var form = jQRSX("#requestForm");

                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        url: '/eShop/Qualification/ValidateCallback',
                        dataType: 'json',
                        data: form.serialize(),
                        success: function (data) {
                            if (data.content == "success") {
                                fillSuccessCallmeBackForm();
                                $('#callmebackrequestsuccess').modal();
                                $('#requestCallback').modal('hide');

                                var lightboxContent = document.getElementById('callmebackrequestsuccess');
                                lightboxContent = $(lightboxContent).text();
                                try {
                                    s_oTrackPage({
                                        s_oAPT: "104-2-1",
                                        s_oPRM: "open, " + FormatLightBoxContent($("#callmebackrequestsuccess").find("h3").text()),
                                        s_oLBC: Formatted_Omniture_LBContent($("#callmebackrequestsuccess").find(".rsx-notificationtoppad").text()),
                                        s_oPLE: Formatted_Omniture_LBContent($("#callmebackrequestsuccess").find(".rsx-pad-v").text())
                                    });
                                }
                                catch (e) {
                                }
                                return false;
                            } else if (data.content == "callbackvalidationerror") {
                                setServerValidationMessages(data.errors);
                            }
                            else if (data.content == "callbackerror") {
                                saveCallbackAddressError();
                            }
                        },
                        error: function (result) {
                            saveCallbackAddressError();
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
            ClearExistingErrors();
        }

        return {
            ClearExistingErrors: ClearExistingErrors,
            Init: init
        }
    }());

    $(document).ready(function () {
        EShop.RequestaCallback.Init();
        EShop.RequestaCallback.ClearExistingErrors();


    });
</script>

    $("#centralQualButton, [id^=centralQualButton], [id^=ckeckavailabilitybtn_], [id^=check_avai_], [id^=checkAvailButton_], [id^=ordernow], #availcheck").on('click', function () {
        let triggerID = "#" + $(this).attr("id");
        let modalId = ""
        //if  modal is triggerd by bootstrap attributes
        if ($(this).attr("data-target")) {
            modalId = $(this).attr("data-target");
        } else if ($(this).attr("onclick").split('\'')[1]) {
            // if triggers by onclick event
            modalId = $(this).attr("onclick").split('\'')[1];
            if (modalId == "fibetvst_i020411") {
                modalId = "#eShopAddressModal1";
            }
        } else {
            modalId = $(this).attr("onclick").split('\"')[1];
        }
        // adding # before if is not there
        if (modalId[0] != "#") {
            modalId = "#" + modalId;
        }
        $(modalId).attr("data-button-trigger", triggerID);
    });
    // all modals that were opened by omniture buttons gets focus back to trigger button.
    $('.modal').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
        if ($(this).attr("data-button-trigger")) {
            $($(this).attr("data-button-trigger")).focus();
            $(this).removeAttr("data-button-trigger");
        }
    });

    <script>
        // --- start CR86005 ---
        function getCookie(cname) {
            let name = cname + "=";
            let ca = document.cookie.split(';');
            for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                let c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                    c = c.substring(1);
                }
                if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                }
            }
            return "";
        }
        function getPromoCodeForGreenFieldByProduct(promoCode, productId) {
            var PromoCode = promoCode;
            let IsGreenFieldAddressCookie = getCookie("IsGreenFieldAddress");
            var prov = $("meta[name=province]").attr("content");

            if (IsGreenFieldAddressCookie.toLowerCase() == "true" && prov == "ON" &&
                (productId == "157eaf02-a740-4bfe-8d20-ab09edb3a0f1"
                    || productId == "3395d523-b32e-4dd5-817c-8acea2138556"
                    || productId == "09a008b5-e9dc-4c6b-8f03-4ecb30924c3b"
                    || productId == "1ed87064-8bb1-4ec8-9e46-e66304a274a5")) {
                PromoCode = "s1UM7UYs";
            }

            return PromoCode;
        }
        // --- end CR86005 ---

        function generateModalPromo() {
            var productName = $("#qualPrd").val();
            var promoCode = $("#qualPromoCode").val();
            var returnedUrl = $("#returnedURLForProduct").val();
            if (!returnedUrl) {
                returnedUrl = '/Bell_Internet/Internet_access';
            }

            // --- start CR86005 ---
            var productId = $("meta[name=ProductID]").attr("content");
            if (productId != null) {
                promoCode = getPromoCodeForGreenFieldByProduct(promoCode, productId);
            }
            // --- end CR86005 ---

            BELL.shop.internet.BuyWithEncodedPromoCode('DSL', productName, promoCode, returnedUrl, false)
        }
        var oldIntURL = '';
        var newUrl = '';
        $(".qualPrdSet").on("click", function () {
            var promoCode = $("#qualPromoCode").val();
            var intProductName = $(this).data("data-product-shortname");
            var intProductLobName = $(this).data("data-product-lobname");
            if (intProductName !== "" && intProductName !== 'undefined' && intProductName !== undefined && intProductName !== null
                && intProductLobName !== "" && intProductLobName !== 'undefined' && intProductLobName != undefined && intProductLobName !== null) {
                var $link = $('#add_lblfs');
                if (oldIntURL === '' || oldIntURL === 'undefined') {
                    oldIntURL = encodeURIComponent($link.attr("href"));
                }
                if (promoCode !== "" && promoCode !== null) {
                    newUrl = decodeURIComponent(oldIntURL) + "%26LobType=" + intProductLobName + "%26ShortName=" + intProductName + "%26PC=" + promoCode;
                }
                else {
                    newUrl = decodeURIComponent(oldIntURL) + "%26LobType=" + intProductLobName + "%26ShortName=" + intProductName;
                }
                $link.attr("href", newUrl);
            }
        });
    </script>

    <script>
        var oldURL = '';
        var $link = '';
        var newUrl = '';
        $(".qualPrdSet").on("click", function () {
            var promoCode = $("#qualPromoCode").val();
            var qualPrdShortName = $('#qualPrdShortName').val();
            var qualPrdLob = $('#qualPrdLob').val();
            if ((qualPrdShortName !== "" && qualPrdLob !== "") && (qualPrdShortName !== 'undefined' && qualPrdLob !== 'undefined') && (qualPrdShortName !== null && qualPrdLob !== null)) {
                if (qualPrdLob == "SHOP_INTERNET" || qualPrdLob == "FIBE_TV") {
                    $link = $('#add_lblfs');
                }
                else if (qualPrdLob == "SATELLITE_TV") {
                    $link = $('#add_lblfstv');
                }
                if (oldURL === '' || oldURL === 'undefined') {
                    oldURL = encodeURIComponent($link.attr("href"));
                }
                if(promoCode !== "" && promoCode !== null) {
                    newUrl = decodeURIComponent(oldURL) + "%26LobType=" + qualPrdLob + "%26ShortName=" + qualPrdShortName + "%26PC=" + promoCode;
                }
                else {
                    newUrl = decodeURIComponent(oldURL) + "%26LobType=" + qualPrdLob + "%26ShortName=" + qualPrdShortName;
                }
                $link.attr("href", newUrl);
            }
        });
    </script>

<script>
            var recaptchaWindow = null;
            var captchaCounter = 0;
            window.captchaWindow = 0;

            browserDetails = (function () {
                var ua = navigator.userAgent, tem, M = ua.match(/(opera|chrome|safari|firefox|msie|trident(?=\/))\/?\s*(\d+)/i) || [];
                if (/trident/i.test(M[1])) {
                    tem = /\brv[ :]+(\d+)/g.exec(ua) || [];
                    return { name: "MSIE", version: (tem[1] || "") };
                }
                if (M[1] === "Chrome") {
                    tem = ua.match(/\b(OPR|Edge)\/(\d+)/);
                    if (tem != null) {
                        return { name: tem[1].replace("OPR", "Opera"), version: tem[2] };
                    }
                }
                M = M[2] ? [M[1], M[2]] : [navigator.appName, navigator.appVersion, "-?"];
                tem = ua.match(/version\/(\d+)/i);
                if (tem != null) {
                    M.splice(1, 1, tem[1]);
                }
                return { name: M[0], version: M[1] };
            }());

    function init(tagName, key) {
                try {
                    captchaId = grecaptcha.render(tagName, {
                        'sitekey': key,
                        'callback': successCaptchaCallback,
                        'size': 'invisible',
                        'badge': 'inline',
                        'error-callback': errorCaptchaCallback
                    });
                } catch (err) {
                    console.error("reCAPTCHA init failed: ", err);
                }
                setTimeout(showCaptchaUnsupported(tagName), 100);
            }

    function initWithCallback(tagName, key, callback) {
                var id = -1;
                try {
                    id = grecaptcha.render(tagName, {
                        'sitekey': key,
                        'callback': callback,
                        'size': 'invisible',
                        'badge': 'inline',
                        'error-callback': errorCaptchaCallback
                    });
                } catch (err) {
                    //alert(err);
                }
                setTimeout(showCaptchaUnsupported(tagName), 100);
                return id;
            }


            function isIEInCompatibleMode() {
                return !!~navigator.userAgent.search(/compatible/g);
            }

            function successCaptchaCallback(token) {
                captchaCallback(token);
            }

            function errorCaptchaCallback(err) {
                errorCallback(err);
            }


            function setBrowserUrl() {
                var browserName = browserDetails.name;


                var url = "#";
                switch (browserName) {
                    case "MSIE":
                        url = "urlie";
                        break;
                    case "Chrome":
                        url = "urlchrome";
                        break;
                    case "Firefox":
                        url = "urlmoz";
                        break;
                    case "Safari":
                        url = "urlsafari";
                        break;
                }
                setCustomBrowserUpgradeBtn(url);

            }

    function executeCaptcha() {
        
                if ("MutationObserver" in window) {
                    if (window.recaptchaListener == null) {
                        window.recaptchaListener = true;
                        HTMLCollection.prototype.find = Array.prototype.find;
                        var captchaFrame = jQuery("iframe[src*='https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api2/bframe']")
                        if (captchaFrame.length > 0) {
                            //recaptchaWindow = document.getElementsByTagName('iframe').find(x => x.getAttribute("title") != null && x.getAttribute("title").includes('challenge')).parentNode.parentNode;
                            recaptchaWindow = captchaFrame[0].parentNode.parentNode;
                            window.recaptchaListener = new MutationObserver(onCaptchaChange);
                            window.recaptchaListener.observe(recaptchaWindow, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['style'] });
                            recaptchaWindow.lastElementChild.className = "rsx-captcha-window position-fixed";
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        var captchaFrame = jQuery("iframe[src*='https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api2/bframe']")
                        if (captchaFrame.length > 0) {
                            //recaptchaWindow = document.getElementsByTagName('iframe').find(x => x.getAttribute("title") != null && x.getAttribute("title").includes('challenge')).parentNode.parentNode;
                            recaptchaWindow = captchaFrame[0].parentNode.parentNode;
                            window.recaptchaListener.observe(recaptchaWindow, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['style'] });
                            recaptchaWindow.lastElementChild.className = "rsx-captcha-window position-fixed";
                        }
                    }
                }
                grecaptcha.execute(captchaId);
            }

	    function executeCaptchaWithId(id) {
                if ("MutationObserver" in window) {
                    if (window.recaptchaListener == null) {
                        window.recaptchaListener = true;
                        HTMLCollection.prototype.find = Array.prototype.find;
                        var captchaFrame = jQuery("iframe[src*='https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api2/bframe']")
                        if (captchaFrame.length > 0) {
                            //recaptchaWindow = document.getElementsByTagName('iframe').find(x => x.getAttribute("title") != null && x.getAttribute("title").includes('challenge')).parentNode.parentNode;
                            recaptchaWindow = captchaFrame[0].parentNode.parentNode;
                            window.recaptchaListener = new MutationObserver(onCaptchaChange);
                            window.recaptchaListener.observe(recaptchaWindow, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['style'] });
                            recaptchaWindow.lastElementChild.className = "rsx-captcha-window position-fixed";
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        var captchaFrame = jQuery("iframe[src*='https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api2/bframe']")
                        if (captchaFrame.length > 0) {
                            //recaptchaWindow = document.getElementsByTagName('iframe').find(x => x.getAttribute("title") != null && x.getAttribute("title").includes('challenge')).parentNode.parentNode;
                            recaptchaWindow = captchaFrame[0].parentNode.parentNode;
                            window.recaptchaListener.observe(recaptchaWindow, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['style'] });
                            recaptchaWindow.lastElementChild.className = "rsx-captcha-window position-fixed";
                        }
                    }
                }
                grecaptcha.execute(id);
            }

            function onCaptchaChange() {

                if (recaptchaWindow != null) {
                    if (recaptchaWindow.style.opacity == 1) {
                        if (window.captchaWindow == 0) {
                            captchaCounter++;
                            onChange();
                        }
                        window.captchaWindow = 1;
                    }
                    else if (recaptchaWindow.style.opacity == 0) {
                        window.captchaWindow = 0;
                    }

                }
    }

    function validateCaptchaV3(token, actionname) {
        // called if success               
        var url = "/ajax/Toolbox/ValidateCaptchaV3";
        jQuery.ajax({
            type: 'POST',
            url: url,
            cache: false,
            async: true,
            data: { captcha : token, action: actionname },
            success: function (data) {
                console.log("captcha validated");
            },
            error: function () {
                console.log("captcha validation failed");
            }
        });
    }

    function executeCaptchaV3Score(callback) {
        grecaptcha.ready(function () {
            grecaptcha.execute('6LdubqkUAAAAAAWt2ytLbsUHuQtisp076hU_nbpc', { action: actionname }).then(function (token) {
                var url = "/ajax/Toolbox/ValidateCaptchaV3WithScore";
                return jQuery.ajax({
                    type: 'POST',
                    url: url,
                    cache: false,
                    async: false,
                    data: { captcha: token, action: actionname },
                    success: callback,
                    error: function () {
                        console.log("captcha validation failed");
                    }
                }, callback);
            });
        });
    }

    <script defer="">
        var captchaId = -1;
        var unsupported = -1;
        var callbackfunc = null;
        var actionname = "Shop_Qualification";

        function errorCallback() {}

        function setCustomBrowserUpgradeBtn(url) {
            if (url != "#") {
                jQuery('#captchaUpgradeBrowserBtn').attr("href", jQuery('#captchaUpgradeBrowserBtn').data(url));
                jQuery('#errorcaptchaUpgradeBrowserBtn').attr("href", jQuery('#errorcaptchaUpgradeBrowserBtn').data(url));
            }
        }

        function showCustomUnsupported() {
            unsupported = 1;
            document.getElementById("captchaDeprecated").style.display = "block";
            //document.getElementById("deprecatedBrowserJs").style.display = "none";
        }

        function onChange() {
            s_oTrackPage({
                s_oAPT: "002-0-0"
            });
            //console.log("change");
            //jQuery('#counter').html(captchaCounter);
        }

        function processCaptchaCallback(callback) {
            callbackfunc = callback;
            initCaptcha();
            if ("True".toLowerCase() === "true") {
                executeCaptchaV3Score(function (data) {
                    if (data.success) {
                        console.log("Executing V2");
                        executeOnCaptchaReady(executeCaptcha);
                    } else {
                        captchaCallback("");
                    }
                });
            }
            else {
                executeOnCaptchaReady(executeCaptcha);
            }
        }

        function processCaptcha() {
            if (unsupported == 1) {}
            else {
                if ("True".toLowerCase() === "true") {
                    executeCaptchaV3();
                }
                initCaptcha();
                executeOnCaptchaReady(executeCaptcha);
            }
        }

        function captchaCallbackv3() {}

        function captchaCallback(token) {
            grecaptcha.reset(captchaId);
            if (callbackfunc != null) {
                callbackfunc(token);
            }
        }

        function initCaptcha() {
            // Initialize Captcha V2
            if (captchaId === -1) {
                init('captchaDiv', '6LdJcEMUAAAAAKfawPudQG0D4ulahlj9s1ECZ7V8');
            }
        }

        function executeOnCaptchaReady(onRecaptchaReadyCallback) {
            // Execute when Captcha V2 ready
            if (onRecaptchaReadyCallback) {
                var cancelV2 = setInterval(function () {
                    console.log('loading recaptcha');
                    if (grecaptcha && captchaId !== -1) {
                        clearInterval(cancelV2);
                        console.log('executing recaptcha');
                        onRecaptchaReadyCallback();
                    }
                }, 200);
            }
        }

    </script>

<script>
    var clickOriginPos;
    var modalLinks = $("[data-toggle='modal'], [role='button'], #manualAddressLink, #centralQualButton, a.checkavail-btn, #availcheck, [tabindex]:not([tabindex='- 1'])");
    $.each(modalLinks, function (i, e) {
        let $this = $(e);
        $this.on("click", function () {
            clickOriginPos = $this;
        });
    });
    $(document).on('shown.bs.modal', '.modal', function (evt) {
        clickOriginPos = (clickOriginPos && clickOriginPos.length > 0) ? $(clickOriginPos) : $(evt.relatedTarget);
        var newModal = $(this);
        $(newModal).keydown(function (e) {
            if ((e.which || e.keyCode) == 27) {
                $(newModal).modal('hide');

                clickOriginPos.focus();
                e.preventDefault();
            }
        });
    });
    $('*[data-dismiss="modal"], button[data-dismiss="modal"], .close').click(function (e) {
        clickOriginPos.focus();
    });

    $(document).on('click', '#addressprovincemodal .accss-address-province-modal-close', function () {
        $('#eShopAddressModal1').modal("show");
        setTimeout(function () {
            $('#ValidationAddressHowtoBuy').focus();
        }, 500);
    });
</script>

<script>
    $(function () {
        const accessiblePcaAutoComplete = {
            // set common properties to be accessed inside each method of this object
            pcaContainer: $('.pcaautocomplete.pcatext:not(.pcacountrylist)').last(),
            pcaInput: $('#ValidationAddressHowtoBuy'),
            liveSuggestions: $('#live-suggestions'),
            highlightedSuggestion: $('#highlighted-suggestion'),
            // initialize on load
            init: function () {
                //check if pca exists in the page, proceed only if there is a pca component in the page
                if (!this.pcaContainer) return;
                // use js observer to watch for changes particularly if the autocomplete pops up or the autocomplete list updates
                const observerConfig = { attributes: false, childList: true, subtree: true, characterData: true };
                const observerCallback = (mutationList, observer) => {
                    // if autocomplete appears, set aria-expanded to true, announce the total number of results and announce the first item as highlighted by adding appropriate text to the aria-live region (#live-suggestions, #highlighted-suggestion)
                    if (this.pcaContainer.is(':visible')) {
                        const result = this.pcaContainer.find('.pcaitem').length > 1 ? `${this.pcaContainer.find('.pcaitem').length} results are available` : `1 result is available`;
                        this.pcaInput.attr('aria-expanded', true)
                        //Add 200ms delay to let the expanded state be announced first by screen reader
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            this.liveSuggestions.text(result)
                            this.highlightedSuggestion.text(`${this.pcaContainer.find('.pcaselected').text()} option 1 of ${this.pcaContainer.find('.pcaitem').length} is highlighted`);
                        }, 200);
                    }
                    else {
                        //else, set the aria expanded to true and set the live regions to empty
                        this.pcaInput.attr('aria-expanded', false)
                        this.liveSuggestions.text('');
                        this.highlightedSuggestion.text('')
                    }
                };
                const observer = new MutationObserver(observerCallback);
                observer.observe(this.pcaContainer.get(0), observerConfig);
                this.setAriaExpanded();
                this.setInputKeyup();
            },
            // sets aria-expanded state whenever the autocomplete appears or disappears
            setAriaExpanded: function () {
                // use observer to watch changes especifically if the autocomplete appears or disappears
                const observerConfig = { attributes: true, childlist: false, subtree: false }
                const observerCallback = (mutationList, observer) => {
                    if (this.pcaContainer.is(':visible')) {
                        this.pcaInput.attr('aria-expanded', true);
                    }
                    else {
                        this.pcaInput.attr('aria-expanded', false);
                        //also clear the aria-live regions when the autocomplete disappears from the screen
                        this.liveSuggestions.text('');
                        this.highlightedSuggestion.text('')
                    }
                }
                const observer = new MutationObserver(observerCallback);
                observer.observe(this.pcaContainer.get(0), observerConfig);
            },
            // set keyup eventhandler
            setInputKeyup: function () {
                const self = this;
                self.pcaInput.on('keyup', function (e) {
                    // clear the live suggestions so that a new result is announced each time
                    self.liveSuggestions.text('');
                    const $this = $(this);
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        $selectedAddress = $('.pcaselected').text();
                        // if arrow up or down key is pressed, set input value to the highlighted suggestion and set #highlighted-suggestion text to whichever is highlighted so that the screen reader will announce its position.
                        if (e.keyCode == 40 || e.keyCode == 38) {
                            let selectedIndex;
                            $this.val($selectedAddress);
                            self.pcaContainer.find('.pcaitem').each(function (index) {
                                if ($(this).hasClass('pcaselected')) {
                                    selectedIndex = index;
                                }
                            });
                            self.highlightedSuggestion.text(`option ${selectedIndex + 1} of ${self.pcaContainer.find('.pcaitem').length} highlighted`);
                            self.liveSuggestions.text('');
                        }
                    });
                    if (e.keyCode == 27) {
                        $this.val('');
                        e.preventDefault();
                        //fix issue where the autocomplete stops working after pressing escape
                        $(this).blur().focus();
                    }
                });
            }
        }
        // call the init mothod to initialize on load
        accessiblePcaAutoComplete.init();
    });
</script>

<script> 
    (function ($) {

        const stripeCloseByMinutes = 30;
        const studentDockBarCloseCookieName = "StudentDockbarClose";

        function mockStripeChatClick(chatId, selector, isAliant) {
            $(selector).on('click', function () {

                if (!isAliant) {
                    $("#" + chatId).find("input[type='image']").trigger('click');
                    $("#" + chatId).find("input[type='image']").trigger('touchstart');
                } else {
                    javascript: openeGainHelp('bell', eglvepid, eglvelang, eglvecountry);
                }
            });
        }


        function wrapChatLink(chatLinkClass) {
            // alert("observe s5");
            if (!($(".stripeChat").hasClass("activatedAliant"))) {
                // alert("observe s6");
                chatLinkClass.wrap("<a href='javascript:void(0)' style='text-decoration:underline;' class='activated'></a>");
                $(".stripeChat").addClass("activatedAliant");
            }

        }

        function observingChatBox(chatBoxId, chatLinkClass, isAliant) {

            if (!($("#" + chatBoxId).find("input[type='image']").length)) { // if the chatbox is not preloaded
                if (!isAliant) {

                    /*Mutation observer - checking if chatbox is available*/
                    var observer = new MutationObserver(function (mutations) {
                        mutations.forEach(function (mutation) {
                            if (mutation.addedNodes.length) {
                                // alert("observe s1");
                                var addedNode = mutation.addedNodes[0];
                                if (addedNode.tagName && addedNode.getAttribute("role") == "button" && addedNode.getAttribute("type") == "image") {

                                    if (!($(".stripeChat").hasClass("activated"))) {
                                        $(".stripeChat").wrap("<a href='javascript:void(0)' style='text-decoration:underline;'></a>");
                                        $(".stripeChat").addClass("activated");
                                    }

                                    mockStripeChatClick(chatBoxId, ".stripeChat", false);
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    });

                    var chatBox = document.getElementById(chatBoxId);
                    if (chatBox !== null) {
                        //  alert("observe s2");
                        observer.observe(chatBox, { childList: true });
                    }

                }

                else {

                    // alert("observe s3");
                    wrapChatLink(chatLinkClass);
                    mockStripeChatClick(chatBoxId, ".stripeChat", true);
                }


            } else {

                // alert("observe s4");
                //  wrapChatLink(chatLinkClass);
                //  mockStripeChatClick(chatBoxId, ".stripeChat", isAliant);
            }

        }
        //global change for stripe closing cookie setup. not displaying dockbar for 30 mins
        try {
            const setCookieByMinutes = (name, value, timeByMinutes) => {
                const date = new Date();
                date.setTime(date.getTime() + (timeByMinutes * 60 * 1000));
                const expires = `expires=${date.toUTCString()}`;
                document.cookie = `${name}=${value};${expires};path=/`;
            };
            const getCookieByName = (cookieName) => {
                const name = `${cookieName}=`;
                const decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
                const cookieArray = decodedCookie.split(';');

                for (let cookie of cookieArray) {
                    while (cookie.charAt(0) === ' ') {
                        cookie = cookie.substring(1);
                    }
                    if (cookie.indexOf(name) === 0) {
                        return cookie.substring(name.length, cookie.length);
                    }
                }
                return "";
            };
            if (getCookieByName(studentDockBarCloseCookieName))
                $("#dockbar").hide();
            else
                $("#dockbar-close").on("click tougchstart", function () {
                    setCookieByMinutes(studentDockBarCloseCookieName, true, stripeCloseByMinutes);
                })

        } catch (ex) {
            console.warn(ex);
        }       

        $(document).ready(function (e) {
            /**
             * Global variable definition
             */
            var curProv = $(".footer-header-current-province").text().trim();
            if (curProv == "") { curProv = $(".rsx-footer-header-current-province").text().trim(); }
            var allAlaintProvs = ['NB', 'NL', 'NS', 'PE'];

            try {
                var chatBoxId = "inqC2CImgContainer_AnchoredB";
                var isAliant = allAlaintProvs.indexOf(curProv) != -1 ? true : false;
                observingChatBox(chatBoxId, $(".stripeChat"), isAliant);
            }
            catch (ex) {
                // Nothing to show, just handle the error
            }
        });
    }(jQuery))
</script>

                needToRemoveTVLegal = false;
